***сыпать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сыпать.html>сы́пать</a> (8437)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">сꙑпати</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sypati</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*sỳpati</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to pour, strew</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сыпать.html>сы́пать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sýpatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:насыпать.html>насы́пать</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:посыпать.html>посы́пать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">also figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to pour <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of friable/solid objects, such as sand; not liquids</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:сыпать.html>сы́пать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:острота.html>остро́тами</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>sýpatʹ</b> ostrótami</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to witticize</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:сыпать.html>сы́пать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:соль.html>соль</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:рана.html>ра́ну</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>sýpatʹ</b> solʹ na ránu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to pour salt on the wound, to rub it in</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to squander
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:сыпать.html>сы́пать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:деньги.html>де́ньгами</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>sýpatʹ</b> dénʹgami</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to squander money</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b>сы́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>пать</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 6a^.     <a href = vnd.unilang:встречаться.html>Встреча́ются</a> разг. <a href = vnd.unilang:форма.html>фо́рмы</a> <i><a href = vnd.unilang:сыпать.html>сы́пешь</a></i>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:сыпать.html>сы́пет</a></i>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:сыпать.html>сы́пят</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> т. д., <a href = vnd.unilang:стихийный.html>стихи́йно</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:образованный.html>образо́ванные</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> 5-й <a href = vnd.unilang:схема.html>схе́ме</a> спряжения, <a href = vnd.unilang:однако.html>одна́ко</a> орфографически <a href = vnd.unilang:сохранивший.html>сохрани́вшие</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:черта.html>черты́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:написание.html>написа́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> -е- <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́нии</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующего</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́ла</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:нет.html>нет</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-сып-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:понимать.html>-а</a></b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.
</p>

***сыпаться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сыпаться.html>сы́паться</a> (6128)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сыпать.html>сы́пать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sýpatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сыпаться.html>сы́паться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sýpatʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">насы́паться</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:посыпаться.html>посы́паться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to fall, to pour, to run out
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:штукатурка.html>штукату́рка</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:сыпаться.html>сы́плется</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">štukatúrka <b>sýpletsja</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">the plaster flakes off</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to rain down, to pour forth
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:сыпаться.html>сы́паться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:град.html>гра́дом</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>sýpatʹsja</b> grádom</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to hail <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">precipitation</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>, <span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to rain down</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to fall thick and fast
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:удар.html>уда́ры</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:сыпаться.html>сыпа́лись</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:град.html>гра́дом</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">udáry <b>sypálisʹ</b> grádom</i> ― <span class="e-translation">blows were raining down (falling thick and fast)</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <i>(of cloth)</i> to fray out</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to flunk, to fail</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сыпать.html>сы́пать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sýpatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***сырой.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сырой.html>сыро́й</a> (2376)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*syrъ</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*SúHros</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">sour, salty, bitter</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, whence English <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">sour</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сырой.html>сыро́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">syrój</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)сыре́е</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)<a href = vnd.unilang:сырье.html>сыре́й</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>damp, moist</li>
<li>raw, uncooked, unbaked</li>
<li>crude</li>
<li>green, unripe</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:влажный.html>вла́жный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">vlážnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-сыр-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ой</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">endearing diminutive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сырой.html>сыр</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">syr</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">cheese</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сырьевой.html>сырьево́й</a> (15962)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сырье.html>сырьё</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">syrʹjó</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ево́й</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-evój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сырьевой.html>сырьево́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">syrʹjevój</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> raw material
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:сырьевой.html>сырьево́й</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:алмаз.html>алма́з</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>syrʹjevój</b> almáz</i> ― <span class="e-translation">rough diamond</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally"><b>raw material</b> diamond</span>”)</div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><b>сыс<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ка́ть</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 6c.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующие</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́лы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:искать.html>иска́ть</a>, сыскивать.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:приставка.html>Приста́вка</a>: <b>с-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>ко́рень</a>: <b>-ыск-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:понимать.html>-а</a></b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сыскной.html>сыскно́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sysknój</span>) (<i>no comparative</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> detective
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:сыскной.html>сыскно́е</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:агентство.html>аге́нтство</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>sysknóje</b> agéntstvo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">private detective agency</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сыч.html>сыч</a> (16411)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(This etymology is missing or incomplete. Please add to it, or discuss it at the Etymology scriptorium.)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сыч.html>сыч</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">syč</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сыч.html>сыча́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сыч.html>сычи́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сыч.html>сыче́й</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>an owl of genus <i>Athene</i> or <i>Aegolius</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:домовый.html>домо́вый</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:сыч.html>сыч</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">domóvyj <b>syč</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">(<i>Athene noctua</i>) little owl</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">мохноно́гий <b><a href = vnd.unilang:сыч.html>сыч</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">moxnonógij <b>syč</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">(<i>Aegolius funereus</i>) boreal owl</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">poetic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> owl (any bird of the order <i>Strigiformes</i>)</li>
<li>reclusive person</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сыщик.html>сы́щик</a> (8148)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">сы(ска́ть)</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sy(skátʹ)</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-щик</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ščik</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сыщик.html>сы́щик</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sýščik</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сыщик.html>сы́щика</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сыщик.html>сы́щики</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сыщик.html>сы́щиков</a></b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">сы́щица</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>detective, investigator</li>
<li>sleuth, bloodhound, snoop; plain-clothes policeman</li></ol>

</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сюжетный.html>сюже́тный</a> (19630)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сюжет.html>сюже́т</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sjužét</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сюжетный.html>сюже́тный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sjužétnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> story</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> scene</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> plot</li>
<li>having a strong plot</li></ol>
